Goal Preservation of Invariant (file /home/wgy/algorithms/Result/acsl-algorithms/deepseek/deepseek-chat-v3-0324/_prefix_function.c/_prefix_function_verified_final_attempt_13.c, line 23):
Let x = -j.
Let x_1 = Mchar_0[shift_sint8(s, 1 + i + k - j)].
Let x_2 = Mchar_0[shift_sint8(s, k)].
Assume {
  Type: is_sint32(i) /\ is_sint32(j) /\ is_sint32(k) /\ is_sint32(1 + k) /\
      is_sint8(x_2) /\ is_sint8(x_1).
  (* Heap *)
  Type: (region(s.base) <= 0) /\ linked(Malloc_0) /\ sconst(Mchar_0).
  (* Goal *)
  When: (0 <= i_1) /\ (i_1 <= k).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: valid_rd(Malloc_0, s, 1).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: valid_rw(Malloc_0, shift_sint8(s, 0), 1 + i).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: (0 < j) /\ (j <= i).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: 0 < i.
  (* Invariant *)
  Have: (k <= j) /\ (0 <= k).
  (* Invariant *)
  Have: forall i_2 : Z. ((0 <= i_2) -> ((i_2 < k) ->
      (Mchar_0[shift_sint8(s, 1 + i + i_2 - j)]
         = Mchar_0[shift_sint8(s, i_2)]))).
  (* Then *)
  Have: k < j.
  (* Then *)
  Have: x_1 = x_2.
  (* Invariant *)
  Have: (-1) <= k.
}
Prove: Mchar_0[shift_sint8(s, 1 + i + i_1 - j)]
         = Mchar_0[shift_sint8(s, i_1)].
